< Review>
I've been to this plaza less than 5x.  I did not know a taqueria is located here.  It was a Friday and I promised Tess I would get her poke for dinner.  I knew Gavin and I would get Mexican but I didn't know from where.  I wanted to get the poke out of the way first but serendipity presented itself when we parked.  Flamingo's was 3-4 doors down from poke.  SCORE!

Gavin ordered a regular chicken burrito and I ordered the chile verde and super nachos.  I can't speak for Gavin but he enjoyed both halves of his burritos, no complaints whatsoever.  I inhaled the chile verde that same evening; the pork was tender and paired perfectly w/ their fluffy rice!  I did not like the super nachos... the top of the nachos was good but once you've eaten everything at the top, the rest was rather dry and flavorless.

Skip the nachos.  Get the chile verde.

They have outdoor dining as well.</Review>

<name>Jenae Lien< /name><time>1500163573727< /time><Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
Do not let the placement of this place throw you off from quality. Set in a mall food court, this place tops Gaby's and other Mediterranean restaurants near by.

You can order a whole grilled mackerel.

Their salmon falls apart as you bite into it. My mouth was in shock as I am used to tough salmon from kebab houses.

Got the Greek salad, delicious if you like tang and zest as their dressing is has a. delightful light balsamic taste with added blended olives.

Prepare to wait about 15 minutes for your food. Each dish is prepared with each order. The meat is grilled fresh where you can see it.

Take home spices and hot sauces available.<//Review>

Two things I love... tangy and spicy. One other that I‚Äôve recently added: healthy. Ive been doing my best to avoid the typical junk that I put in my body so I tried something a little different. This place is pretty good. The menu pictures will make your mouth water. A lot to choose from. The salad bar looked so so but the tomato and cucumber salad was delicious! One bite and I was in love. I would‚Äôve bought a whole container of it! Very light and refreshing taste. The chicken kabob that I ordered was tasty. Nothing to die for. < Review>
I came in on Friday and decided to go with the chicken salad with a side of hummus.  I would say that for what I got, the cost is moderately priced.  Not overly expensive but not economical either.
The lettuce was pretty bland, definitely not enough dressing to really flavor the dish. The chicken was good though.  Hummus was ok.  The pita was pretty stiff. If anything I would suggest heating up the pita or making it fresh for the guests and adding additional items to the salad to make it interesting. There were some tomatoes, olives etc but the salad seem to be just thrown together with out any sort of real interest.
Service was unfriendly and the order took a long time.
On a plus side they give you a order device that vibrates when your order is ready.  It took about 20 minutes for a chicken salad with one person in front of me and they didnt seem too busy but thats an outsider prospective.< /Review>

< review>
I eat here once in a while. Today I had two shrimp tacos and (my Favorite) two al pastor tacos. As always, chips are gratis, and the salsa bar is outstanding. I always order the tacos here, because they are the most-authentic street tacos I have found in this area. They have it all, including cabeza, lengua, and buche; not to mention the usual asada, al pastor, pollo, and carnitas. Although I almost always order the tacos, they also make a killer burrito. If you love Mexican food, you have to try Taqueria Guerrero.</review>

<Pictures>None</Pictures>< review>
Do yourself a favor, reserve a storage unit HERE!

Not only does it include amazing customer service by friendly, professional staff but it's also an affordable price for LA in a navigable location. Don't forget the convenience of managing your account online while having a flexible month to month contract :)

Obviously everyone knows that moving is stressful. My move was especially stressful, not because the fact I was moving from San Diego, but everything that you think could and couldn't go wrong...went wrong. From broken boxes from accident prone movers and sitting in traffic with empty gas tanks to wrong keys by missing landlords and ruined newly bought furniture and mishandled sentimental belongings- I begged the day to be over and naturally I dreaded my last stop:storage. It was heaven- the exact opposite of how my day was going.
Seriously I'm considering to believe in angels because when I went there, I easily spotted and found parking right away. I was greeted sincerely and helped right away! They worked with the movers and everything was stored and moved unbelievably smoothly! Words cannot express my gratitude and satisfaction. Thank you so much Stanley and Yesenia, I highly recommend you to go to this Public Storage unit!!< /review>
